         from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, redirect, url_for, session
         import os
         import csv
         import threading
         import datetime
         import uuid
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'supersecretkey'
         
         # File path constants
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         ARTICLES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt')
         ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'article_versions.txt')
         APPROVALS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'approvals.txt')
         CALENDAR_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'calendar.txt')
         
         lock = threading.Lock()
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def generate_uuid():
             return str(uuid.uuid4())
         
         
         def current_timestamp():
             return datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + 'Z'
         
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filepath):
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return []
             with open(filepath, 'r', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|')
                 return list(reader)
         
         
         def write_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, data, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     writer.writeheader()
                     for row in data:
                         writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, row, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 file_exists = os.path.exists(filepath)
                 with open(filepath, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     if not file_exists:
                         writer.writeheader()
                     writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         # Session user retrieval helper
         
         def get_current_username():
             return session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_current_username()
             # Simple summary: List of articles authored by user (from articles.txt) with counts
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a.get('author') == username]
         
             # For each article, count versions and approvals
             article_summaries = []
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
         
             for art in user_articles:
                 aid = art.get('article_id')
                 art_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == aid]
                 art_approvals = [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == aid and a['status'] == 'approved']
                 article_summaries.append({
                     'article_id': aid,
                     'title': art.get('title', ''),
                     'versions_count': len(art_versions),
                     'approved_count': len(art_approvals)
                 })
             context = {
                 'username': username,
                 'my_articles': article_summaries
             }
             return jsonify(context)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return jsonify({'info': 'Send POST with title and content to create article'})
         
             form = request.form
             title = form.get('title')
             content = form.get('content')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not title or not content:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Title and content required'}), 400
         
             article_id = generate_uuid()
         
             # Save article metadata
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             articles.append({'article_id': article_id, 'title': title, 'author': username})
             write_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE, articles, ['article_id', 'title', 'author'])
         
             # Initial version
             version_id = generate_uuid()
             version = {
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_number': '1',
                 'content': content,
                 'username': username,
                 'change_summary': 'Initial version',
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, version, version.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Article created', 'article_id': article_id, 'version_id': version_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             article = next((a for a in articles if a['article_id'] == article_id), None)
             if article is None:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Article not found'}), 404
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
                 version_history = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
                 version_history.sort(key=lambda x: int(x['version_number']))
                 return jsonify({'article': article, 'version_history': version_history})
         
             # POST updates
             form = request.form
             content = form.get('content')
             change_summary = form.get('change_summary', '')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not content:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Content required for new version'}), 400
         
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
             next_version_num = 1 + max([int(v['version_number']) for v in article_versions], default=0)
         
             version_id = generate_uuid()
             new_version = {
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_number': str(next_version_num),
                 'content': content,
                 'username': username,
                 'change_summary': change_summary,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, new_version, new_version.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Article updated', 'version_id': version_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/mine')
         def my_articles():
             username = get_current_username()
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a.get('author') == username]
             return jsonify({'my_articles': user_articles})
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/published')
         def published_articles():
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
         
             # Filter published articles: if latest version has an approval with approved status
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
             published = []
             for art in articles:
                 aid = art['article_id']
                 article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == aid]
                 if not article_versions:
                     continue
                 latest_version = max(article_versions, key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
         
                 # Check if latest version approved
                 latest_approved = any(a for a in approvals if a['version_id'] == latest_version['version_id'] and a['status'] == 'approved')
                 if latest_approved:
                     published.append({
                         'article_id': aid,
                         'title': art.get('title', ''),
                         'version_number': latest_version['version_number'],
                         'content': latest_version['content'],
                         'approved': True
                     })
             return jsonify({'published_articles': published})
         
         
         @app.route('/calendar', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def calendar():
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 schedule = read_pipe_delimited_file(CALENDAR_FILE)
                 return jsonify({'calendar': schedule})
         
             # POST - add a scheduling entry
             form = request.form
             article_id = form.get('article_id')
             publish_date = form.get('publish_date')  # ISO format expected
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not article_id or not publish_date:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'article_id and publish_date required'}), 400
         
             entry = {
                 'schedule_id': generate_uuid(),
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'publish_date': publish_date,
                 'username': username,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(CALENDAR_FILE, entry, entry.keys())
             return jsonify({'message': 'Schedule entry added', 'schedule_id': entry['schedule_id']})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_article(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             status = form.get('status')  # e.g., approved, rejected, revision_requested
             comment = form.get('comment', '')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id or not status:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and status are required'}), 400
         
             approval_id = generate_uuid()
             approval_entry = {
                 'approval_id': approval_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': status,
                 'comment': comment,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, approval_entry, approval_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval_id': approval_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/comments', methods=['POST'])
         def add_comment(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             comment_text = form.get('comment')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id or not comment_text:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and comment text are required'}), 400
         
             comment_entry = {
                 'approval_id': generate_uuid(),
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': '',
                 'comment': comment_text,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, comment_entry, comment_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Comment added'})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/analytics')
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
         
             article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
             approved_approvals = [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id and a['status'] == 'approved']
         
             analytics = {
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'total_versions': len(article_versions),
                 'approved_versions': len(set(a['version_id'] for a in approved_approvals)),
                 'total_approvals': len([a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id]),
                 'total_comments': len([a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id and not a['status']]),
             }
             return jsonify(analytics)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)
             app.run(debug=True)

         import os
         import csv
         import threading
         import datetime
         import uuid
         from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, redirect, url_for, session, render_template
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'supersecretkeyreplace'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         ARTICLES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt')
         ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'article_versions.txt')
         APPROVALS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'approvals.txt')
         COMMENTS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'comments.txt')
         WORKFLOW_STAGES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'workflow_stages.txt')
         
         lock = threading.Lock()
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def safe_read_pipe_delimited(file_path):
             if not os.path.isfile(file_path):
                 return []
             with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
                 reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|')
                 return list(reader)
         
         
         def safe_write_pipe_delimited(file_path, data, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     writer.writeheader()
                     writer.writerows(data)
         
         
         def safe_append_pipe_delimited(file_path, row, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 file_exists = os.path.isfile(file_path)
                 with open(file_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8', newline='') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     if not file_exists:
                         writer.writeheader()
                     writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         def generate_uuid():
             return str(uuid.uuid4())
         
         
         def get_timestamp():
             return datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + 'Z'
         
         
         def get_current_username():
             return session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
         
         # Models
         class ArticlesModel:
             FIELDS = ['article_id', 'title', 'author', 'category', 'status', 'last_modified']
         
             @staticmethod
             def list_all():
                 return safe_read_pipe_delimited(ARTICLES_FILE)
         
             @staticmethod
             def find_by_id(article_id):
                 articles = ArticlesModel.list_all()
                 for a in articles:
                     if a['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                         return a
                 return None
         
             @staticmethod
             def add(article):
                 articles = ArticlesModel.list_all()
                 articles.append(article)
                 safe_write_pipe_delimited(ARTICLES_FILE, articles, ArticlesModel.FIELDS)
         
             @staticmethod
             def update(article_id, updated_data):
                 articles = ArticlesModel.list_all()
                 updated = False
                 for i, art in enumerate(articles):
                     if art['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                         articles[i].update(updated_data)
                         updated = True
                         break
                 if updated:
                     safe_write_pipe_delimited(ARTICLES_FILE, articles, ArticlesModel.FIELDS)
                 return updated
         
         
         class ArticleVersionsModel:
             FIELDS = ['version_id', 'article_id', 'version_number', 'content', 'author', 'created_date', 'change_summary']
         
             @staticmethod
             def list_all():
                 return safe_read_pipe_delimited(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
         
             @staticmethod
             def find_by_article(article_id):
                 versions = ArticleVersionsModel.list_all()
                 return [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
         
             @staticmethod
             def add(version):
                 safe_append_pipe_delimited(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, version, ArticleVersionsModel.FIELDS)
         
             @staticmethod
             def max_version_number(article_id):
                 versions = ArticleVersionsModel.find_by_article(article_id)
                 if not versions:
                     return 0
                 return max(int(v['version_number']) for v in versions)
         
         
         class ApprovalsModel:
             FIELDS = ['approval_id', 'article_id', 'version_id', 'approver', 'status', 'comments', 'timestamp']
         
             @staticmethod
             def list_all():
                 return safe_read_pipe_delimited(APPROVALS_FILE)
         
             @staticmethod
             def find_by_article(article_id):
                 approvals = ApprovalsModel.list_all()
                 return [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
         
             @staticmethod
             def add(approval):
                 safe_append_pipe_delimited(APPROVALS_FILE, approval, ApprovalsModel.FIELDS)
         
         
         class CommentsModel:
             FIELDS = ['comment_id', 'article_id', 'version_id', 'author', 'comment', 'timestamp']
         
             @staticmethod
             def list_all():
                 return safe_read_pipe_delimited(COMMENTS_FILE)
         
             @staticmethod
             def find_by_version(version_id):
                 comments = CommentsModel.list_all()
                 return [c for c in comments if c['version_id'] == str(version_id)]
         
             @staticmethod
             def add(comment):
                 safe_append_pipe_delimited(COMMENTS_FILE, comment, CommentsModel.FIELDS)
         
         
         # Services
         class ArticleService:
             @staticmethod
             def create_article(title, content, author, category=None):
                 article_id = generate_uuid()
                 now = get_timestamp()
                 article = {
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'title': title,
                     'author': author,
                     'category': category if category else '',
                     'status': 'draft',
                     'last_modified': now
                 }
                 ArticlesModel.add(article)
         
                 version_id = generate_uuid()
                 version_record = {
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_number': '1',
                     'content': content,
                     'author': author,
                     'created_date': now,
                     'change_summary': 'Initial version',
                 }
                 ArticleVersionsModel.add(version_record)
                 return article_id, version_id
         
             @staticmethod
             def edit_article(article_id, content, change_summary, author):
                 article = ArticlesModel.find_by_id(article_id)
                 if not article:
                     return None, 'Article not found.'
                 max_version = ArticleVersionsModel.max_version_number(article_id)
                 next_version_num = max_version + 1
                 now = get_timestamp()
         
                 version_id = generate_uuid()
                 version_record = {
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_number': str(next_version_num),
                     'content': content,
                     'author': author,
                     'created_date': now,
                     'change_summary': change_summary,
                 }
                 ArticleVersionsModel.add(version_record)
                 ArticlesModel.update(article_id, {'last_modified': now})
                 return version_id, None
         
             @staticmethod
             def get_version_history(article_id):
                 versions = ArticleVersionsModel.find_by_article(article_id)
                 versions_sorted = sorted(versions, key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
                 return versions_sorted
         
         
         class ApprovalService:
             @staticmethod
             def approve_version(article_id, version_id, approver, status, comments):
                 valid_statuses = {'approved', 'rejected', 'revision_requested'}
                 if status not in valid_statuses:
                     return 'Invalid status.'
         
                 approval_id = generate_uuid()
                 approval_record = {
                     'approval_id': approval_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'approver': approver,
                     'status': status,
                     'comments': comments,
                     'timestamp': get_timestamp(),
                 }
                 ApprovalsModel.add(approval_record)
                 # Update article status on approval
                 if status == 'approved':
                     ArticlesModel.update(article_id, {'status': 'published'})
                 elif status == 'revision_requested':
                     ArticlesModel.update(article_id, {'status': 'revision requested'})
                 elif status == 'rejected':
                     ArticlesModel.update(article_id, {'status': 'rejected'})
                 return None
         
             @staticmethod
             def get_approvals(article_id):
                 return ApprovalsModel.find_by_article(article_id)
         
         
         class CommentService:
             @staticmethod
             def add_comment(article_id, version_id, author, comment):
                 comment_id = generate_uuid()
                 comment_record = {
                     'comment_id': comment_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'author': author,
                     'comment': comment,
                     'timestamp': get_timestamp(),
                 }
                 CommentsModel.add(comment_record)
         
         
         # Routes
         @app.route('/')
         def root():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_current_username()
             articles = ArticlesModel.list_all()
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a.get('author') == username]
         
             summaries = []
             for art in user_articles:
                 art_id = art['article_id']
                 versions = ArticleVersionsModel.find_by_article(art_id)
                 approvals = ApprovalsModel.find_by_article(art_id)
                 approval_count = sum(1 for a in approvals if a['status'] == 'approved')
                 summaries.append({
                     'article_id': art_id,
                     'title': art.get('title', ''),
                     'versions_count': len(versions),
                     'approved_count': approval_count,
                 })
         
             return jsonify({'username': username, 'articles': summaries})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return render_template('create_article.html')
         
             title = request.form.get('title', '').strip()
             content = request.form.get('content', '').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category', '').strip()
             username = get_current_username()
         
             errors = {}
             if not title:
                 errors['title'] = 'Title is required.'
             if not content:
                 errors['content'] = 'Content is required.'
             if errors:
                 return render_template('create_article.html', errors=errors)
         
             article_id, version_id = ArticleService.create_article(title, content, username, category)
         
             return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))

                 }
                 return render_template('edit_article.html', article=article_display, version_history=versions)

             errors = {}

                 errors['content'] = 'Content is required.'
             if not change_summary:
                 errors['change_summary'] = 'Change summary is required.'
             if errors:
                 versions = ArticleService.get_version_history(article_id)
                 article_display = {

                     'title': article.get('title', ''),
                     'category': article.get('category', ''),
                     'status': article.get('status', 'draft'),
                     'content': content
                 }
                 return render_template('edit_article.html', errors=errors, article=article_display, version_history=versions), 400
         
             version_id, err = ArticleService.edit_article(article_id, content, change_summary, username)
             if err:
                 return render_template('edit_article.html', error=err), 400
         
             return redirect(url_for('edit_article', article_id=article_id))

         @app.route('/articles/published')
         def published_articles():
             articles = ArticlesModel.list_all()
             versions = ArticleVersionsModel.list_all()
             approvals = ApprovalsModel.list_all()
         
             published_list = []
             categories_set = set()
             for art in articles:
                 art_id = art['article_id']
                 art_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == art_id]
                 if not art_versions:
                     continue
         
                 latest_version = max(art_versions, key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
         
                 latest_approvals = [a for a in approvals if a['version_id'] == latest_version['version_id']]
                 if any(a['status'] == 'approved' for a in latest_approvals):
                     categories_set.add(art.get('category', ''))
                     published_list.append({
                         'id': art_id,
                         'title': art.get('title', ''),
                         'category': art.get('category', ''),
                         'published_date': latest_version['created_date'],
                         'version_number': latest_version['version_number'],
                         'content': latest_version['content'],
                     })
         
             selected_category = request.args.get('category', '')
             selected_sort = request.args.get('sort', 'date')
         
             # Filter by category
             if selected_category:
                 published_list = [p for p in published_list if p.get('category') == selected_category]
         
             # Sort
             if selected_sort == 'title':
                 published_list = sorted(published_list, key=lambda x: x['title'])
             else:  # date
                 published_list = sorted(published_list, key=lambda x: x['published_date'], reverse=True)
         
             categories = sorted(filter(None, categories_set))
         
             return render_template('published_articles.html', articles=published_list, categories=categories, selected_category=selected_category, selected_sort=selected_sort)

         def content_calendar():

                         'category': article.get('category', ''),
                         'status': a.get('status', ''),
                     })
         
                 # Default view param
                 view = request.args.get('view', 'month')
                 return render_template('content_calendar.html', schedule=schedule, view=view)

         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/analytics')
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             article = ArticlesModel.find_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 return render_template('article_analytics.html', error='Article not found.', article_id=article_id, analytics=None), 404
         
             versions = ArticleVersionsModel.find_by_article(article_id)
             approvals = ApprovalsModel.find_by_article(article_id)
             comments = CommentsModel.list_all()
         
             version_count = len(versions)
             approval_count = sum(1 for a in approvals if a['status'] == 'approved')
             comment_count = sum(1 for c in comments if c['article_id'] == str(article_id))
         
             analytics = [
                 {'metric': 'Version Count', 'value': version_count},
                 {'metric': 'Approval Count', 'value': approval_count},
                 {'metric': 'Comment Count', 'value': comment_count},
             ]
         
             return render_template('article_analytics.html', article_id=article_id, analytics=analytics)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_version(article_id):
             data = request.form
             version_id = data.get('version_id')
             status = data.get('status')
             comments = data.get('comments', '')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id is required'}), 400
             if not status or status not in {'approved', 'rejected', 'revision_requested'}:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Valid status is required (approved, rejected, revision_requested)'}), 400
         
             error = ApprovalService.approve_version(article_id, version_id, username, status, comments)
             if error:
                 return jsonify({'error': error}), 400
         
             return jsonify({'message': f'Version {version_id} approval recorded.'})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/comments', methods=['POST'])
         def add_comment(article_id):
             data = request.form
             version_id = data.get('version_id')
             comment_text = data.get('comment')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id is required'}), 400
             if not comment_text:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'comment text is required'}), 400
         
             CommentService.add_comment(article_id, version_id, username, comment_text)
             return jsonify({'message': 'Comment added successfully.'})

         from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, redirect, url_for, session
         import os
         import csv
         import threading
         import datetime
         import uuid
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'supersecretkey'
         
         lock = threading.Lock()
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'article_versions.txt')
         APPROVALS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'approvals.txt')
         ARTICLES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt')  # assumed for basic article metadata storage
         
         # Util functions
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filepath):
             data = []
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return data
             with open(filepath, 'r', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|')
                 for row in reader:
                     data.append(row)
             return data
         
         
         def write_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, data, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     writer.writeheader()
                     for row in data:
                         writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, row, fieldnames):
             # Append a single row to file
             with lock:
                 file_exists = os.path.exists(filepath)
                 with open(filepath, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     if not file_exists:
                         writer.writeheader()
                     writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         # Generate unique IDs
         
         def generate_uuid():
             return str(uuid.uuid4())
         
         
         def current_timestamp():
             return datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + 'Z'
         
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root():
             # Redirect root to dashboard
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             # Return session info and summary data, stub implementation
             user = session.get('username', 'guest')
             # For simplicity, list articles and versions count
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             article_summaries = []
             for art in articles:
                 article_id = art.get('article_id')
                 versions = [v for v in read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE) if v['article_id'] == article_id]
                 article_summaries.append({
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'title': art.get('title', ''),
                     'versions_count': len(versions)
                 })
             return jsonify({
                 'session_user': user,
                 'articles': article_summaries
             })
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 form = request.form
                 title = form.get('title')
                 content = form.get('content')
                 author = session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
                 if not title or not content:
                     return jsonify({'error': 'Title and content are required'}), 400
         
                 # Create a new article entry
                 article_id = generate_uuid()
         
                 # Save basic article metadata
                 articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
                 articles.append({'article_id': article_id, 'title': title, 'author': author})
                 write_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE, articles, fieldnames=['article_id', 'title', 'author'])
         
                 # Create initial version
                 version_id = generate_uuid()
                 version_row = {
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_number': '1',
                     'content': content,
                     'username': author,
                     'change_summary': 'Initial version',
                     'timestamp': current_timestamp()
                 }
                 append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, version_row, fieldnames=version_row.keys())
         
                 return jsonify({'message': 'Article created', 'article_id': article_id, 'version_id': version_id})
             else:
                 # For GET, we only return a placeholder as no frontend templates
                 return jsonify({'info': 'Send POST request with title and content to create article'})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             article = next((a for a in articles if a['article_id'] == article_id), None)
             if article is None:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Article not found'}), 404
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 form = request.form
                 content = form.get('content')
                 change_summary = form.get('change_summary', '')
                 username = session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
                 if not content:
                     return jsonify({'error': 'Content is required to create a new version'}), 400
         
                 # Load versions to determine next version number
                 versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
                 article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
                 if article_versions:
                     max_version = max(int(v['version_number']) for v in article_versions)
                     next_version = max_version + 1
                 else:
                     next_version = 1
         
                 version_id = generate_uuid()
                 new_version = {
                     'version_id': version_id,
                     'article_id': article_id,
                     'version_number': str(next_version),
                     'content': content,
                     'username': username,
                     'change_summary': change_summary,
                     'timestamp': current_timestamp()
                 }
                 append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, new_version, fieldnames=new_version.keys())
         
                 return jsonify({'message': 'Article version updated', 'version_id': version_id})
             else:
                 # For GET, return article data and version history
                 versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
                 version_history = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
                 version_history.sort(key=lambda x: int(x['version_number']))
                 return jsonify({
                     'article': article,
                     'version_history': version_history
                 })
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_article(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             status = form.get('status')  # e.g. approved, rejected
             comment = form.get('comment', '')
             username = session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
             if not version_id or not status:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and status are required'}), 400
         
             # Store approval entry
             approval_id = generate_uuid()
             approval_entry = {
                 'approval_id': approval_id,
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': status,
                 'comment': comment,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, approval_entry, fieldnames=approval_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval_id': approval_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/comments', methods=['POST'])
         def add_comment(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             comment_text = form.get('comment')
             username = session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
             if not version_id or not comment_text:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and comment text are required'}), 400
         
             # Append comment to approvals with a comment type but status empty
             comment_entry = {
                 'approval_id': generate_uuid(),
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': '',
                 'comment': comment_text,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, comment_entry, fieldnames=comment_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Comment added'})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/analytics')
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             # Stub analytics response - could provide views, unique visitors, approval stats
             # For now just count versions and approvals
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             version_count = len([v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id])
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
             approval_count = len([a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id and a['status'] == 'approved'])
         
             return jsonify({
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_count': version_count,
                 'approved_count': approval_count
             })
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             # Ensure data directory exists
             os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, redirect, url_for, session
         import os
         import csv
         import threading
         import datetime
         import uuid
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'supersecretkey'
         
         # File path constants
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         ARTICLES_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'articles.txt')
         ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'article_versions.txt')
         APPROVALS_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'approvals.txt')
         CALENDAR_FILE = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'calendar.txt')
         
         lock = threading.Lock()
         
         # Utility functions
         
         def generate_uuid():
             return str(uuid.uuid4())
         
         
         def current_timestamp():
             return datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + 'Z'
         
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filepath):
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return []
             with open(filepath, 'r', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 reader = csv.DictReader(f, delimiter='|')
                 return list(reader)
         
         
         def write_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, data, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     writer.writeheader()
                     for row in data:
                         writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filepath, row, fieldnames):
             with lock:
                 file_exists = os.path.exists(filepath)
                 with open(filepath, 'a', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     writer = csv.DictWriter(f, fieldnames=fieldnames, delimiter='|')
                     if not file_exists:
                         writer.writeheader()
                     writer.writerow(row)
         
         
         # Session user retrieval helper
         
         def get_current_username():
             return session.get('username', 'anonymous')
         
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_current_username()
             # Simple summary: List of articles authored by user (from articles.txt) with counts
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a.get('author') == username]
         
             # For each article, count versions and approvals
             article_summaries = []
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
         
             for art in user_articles:
                 aid = art.get('article_id')
                 art_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == aid]
                 art_approvals = [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == aid and a['status'] == 'approved']
                 article_summaries.append({
                     'article_id': aid,
                     'title': art.get('title', ''),
                     'versions_count': len(art_versions),
                     'approved_count': len(art_approvals)
                 })
             context = {
                 'username': username,
                 'my_articles': article_summaries
             }
             return jsonify(context)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return jsonify({'info': 'Send POST with title and content to create article'})
         
             form = request.form
             title = form.get('title')
             content = form.get('content')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not title or not content:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Title and content required'}), 400
         
             article_id = generate_uuid()
         
             # Save article metadata
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             articles.append({'article_id': article_id, 'title': title, 'author': username})
             write_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE, articles, ['article_id', 'title', 'author'])
         
             # Initial version
             version_id = generate_uuid()
             version = {
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_number': '1',
                 'content': content,
                 'username': username,
                 'change_summary': 'Initial version',
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, version, version.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Article created', 'article_id': article_id, 'version_id': version_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             article = next((a for a in articles if a['article_id'] == article_id), None)
             if article is None:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Article not found'}), 404
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
                 version_history = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
                 version_history.sort(key=lambda x: int(x['version_number']))
                 return jsonify({'article': article, 'version_history': version_history})
         
             # POST updates
             form = request.form
             content = form.get('content')
             change_summary = form.get('change_summary', '')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not content:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'Content required for new version'}), 400
         
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
             next_version_num = 1 + max([int(v['version_number']) for v in article_versions], default=0)
         
             version_id = generate_uuid()
             new_version = {
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_number': str(next_version_num),
                 'content': content,
                 'username': username,
                 'change_summary': change_summary,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE, new_version, new_version.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Article updated', 'version_id': version_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/mine')
         def my_articles():
             username = get_current_username()
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a.get('author') == username]
             return jsonify({'my_articles': user_articles})
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/published')
         def published_articles():
             articles = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLES_FILE)
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
         
             # Filter published articles: if latest version has an approval with approved status
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
             published = []
             for art in articles:
                 aid = art['article_id']
                 article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == aid]
                 if not article_versions:
                     continue
                 latest_version = max(article_versions, key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
         
                 # Check if latest version approved
                 latest_approved = any(a for a in approvals if a['version_id'] == latest_version['version_id'] and a['status'] == 'approved')
                 if latest_approved:
                     published.append({
                         'article_id': aid,
                         'title': art.get('title', ''),
                         'version_number': latest_version['version_number'],
                         'content': latest_version['content'],
                         'approved': True
                     })
             return jsonify({'published_articles': published})
         
         
         @app.route('/calendar', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def calendar():
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 schedule = read_pipe_delimited_file(CALENDAR_FILE)
                 return jsonify({'calendar': schedule})
         
             # POST - add a scheduling entry
             form = request.form
             article_id = form.get('article_id')
             publish_date = form.get('publish_date')  # ISO format expected
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not article_id or not publish_date:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'article_id and publish_date required'}), 400
         
             entry = {
                 'schedule_id': generate_uuid(),
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'publish_date': publish_date,
                 'username': username,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(CALENDAR_FILE, entry, entry.keys())
             return jsonify({'message': 'Schedule entry added', 'schedule_id': entry['schedule_id']})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_article(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             status = form.get('status')  # e.g., approved, rejected, revision_requested
             comment = form.get('comment', '')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id or not status:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and status are required'}), 400
         
             approval_id = generate_uuid()
             approval_entry = {
                 'approval_id': approval_id,
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': status,
                 'comment': comment,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, approval_entry, approval_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval_id': approval_id})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/comments', methods=['POST'])
         def add_comment(article_id):
             form = request.form
             version_id = form.get('version_id')
             comment_text = form.get('comment')
             username = get_current_username()
         
             if not version_id or not comment_text:
                 return jsonify({'error': 'version_id and comment text are required'}), 400
         
             comment_entry = {
                 'approval_id': generate_uuid(),
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'version_id': version_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'status': '',
                 'comment': comment_text,
                 'timestamp': current_timestamp()
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE, comment_entry, comment_entry.keys())
         
             return jsonify({'message': 'Comment added'})
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<string:article_id>/analytics')
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             versions = read_pipe_delimited_file(ARTICLE_VERSIONS_FILE)
             approvals = read_pipe_delimited_file(APPROVALS_FILE)
         
             article_versions = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == article_id]
             approved_approvals = [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id and a['status'] == 'approved']
         
             analytics = {
                 'article_id': article_id,
                 'total_versions': len(article_versions),
                 'approved_versions': len(set(a['version_id'] for a in approved_approvals)),
                 'total_approvals': len([a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id]),
                 'total_comments': len([a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == article_id and not a['status']]),
             }
             return jsonify(analytics)
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             os.makedirs(DATA_DIR, exist_ok=True)
             app.run(debug=True)
